3077<p>

3078Lauren is an avid DIYer and interior design enthusiast who&rsquo;s spent the last year documenting her home renovation on Instagram <a href="https://www.instagram.com/farmhouseish/">

3079@farmhouseish</a>

3080. Though Lauren had already successfully upgraded other parts of her home, her latest project&mdash;remodeling her entire bathroom&mdash;was the most extensive renovation yet.</p>

3081

3082

3083<p>

3084For that reason, Lauren reached out to our <a href="https://design.vevano.com/design-services/">

3085Vevano Home designers</a>

3086 for help planning the fine details and making her dream modern farmhouse bathroom come to life.</p>

3141<h2>

3142Before</h2>

3143

3144</div>

3145</div>

3146</div>

3147</div>

3148<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-dfed-cba-b-ab-adcc">

3149<div>

3150<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3151<div>

3152<p>

3153Lauren describes her style as &ldquo;<a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/home-interior-style-farmhouse-design/">

3154modern farmhouse</a>

3155 meets <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/home-interior-styles-bohemian-design/">

3156boho</a>

3157&rdquo; and prefers lighter colors and a clean, modern aesthetic. Her original main bathroom leaned more Tuscan and traditional, featuring dark, mahogany-looking wood, bell-shaped lights, and ornately framed mirrors hung over the granite countertops. Everything was far from the modern farmhouse look she wanted.</p>

3217From a functional standpoint, Lauren wanted to keep the beautiful walk-in shower but didn&rsquo;t like that there wasn&rsquo;t a bathtub. Though the existing setup had floor-to-ceiling cabinets and ample storage, her family didn&rsquo;t use all the cabinet space.</p>

3218

3220<p>

3221&ldquo;Our original bathroom simply didn&rsquo;t bring us joy,&rdquo; Lauren says. &ldquo;It didn&rsquo;t fit our needs. And it was the room that we started and ended our days in! We knew it needed to be updated so it could be more functional for us and feel like ours.&rdquo;</p>

3250The Design Process</h2>

3252</div>

3253</div>

3277<div>

3278<h3>

3279Initial Consultation with Vevano Home Designer Martha</h3>

3280

3281

3282<p>

3283Lauren was paired with Vevano Home designer Martha for this bathroom remodel. Martha has extensive expertise in home remodels, including bathrooms, and knew exactly how to help Lauren&nbsp;achieve a modern farmhouse bathroom. In their initial consultation, Lauren and Martha brainstormed the fixtures and upgrades that would meet the modern farmhouse style.</p>

3284

3285

3286<p>

3287Lauren&rsquo;s top priority was to fill the space with bright and airy elements rather than keeping the darker elements in the original layout. Lauren also wanted less storage, suggesting that they remove the floor-to-ceiling cabinets, allowing room for a tiled look along the back wall behind the new vanity. She still wanted double sinks in the vanity, but she wanted a simpler design with modern lighting and minimalist mirrors.</p>

3288

3289

3290<p>

3291Next on Lauren&rsquo;s wish list was to make significant upgrades to the shower and bathtub&mdash;which meant creating space for a bathtub that didn&rsquo;t even exist yet! Since she only has one other bathtub in her home, she hoped they could find space for a freestanding bathtub by removing the tall cabinets and moving the vanity over. Lauren was already happy with her walk-in shower, so all she wanted to do was paint the existing tile white to match the other bright elements she hoped to add.</p>

3292

3293

3294<p>

3295After hearing Lauren&rsquo;s ideas, Martha asked clarifying questions to help complete her notes before starting on the concept board. Though Lauren tends to choose white cabinets and other pieces throughout her home, Martha explained how a darker-colored vanity could complement the light interior of the bathroom. They also talked through tub ideas and how they could work with the current layout.</p>

3296

3297

3298<p>

3299&ldquo;At first, I was worried about the layout, what our options were, and what would look best where,&rdquo; Lauren says. &ldquo;Talking through those worries initially with Martha was very helpful!&rdquo;</p>

3300

3327<h3>

3328Developing Concept Boards</h3>

3329

3330

3331<p>

3332Once Martha had enough details from her conversation with Lauren, it was time to draft the concept boards. Lauren had already chosen a white and grey oriental-style floor tile and a light grey, hexagonal tile for the wall behind the vanity. Martha made sure to match all the fixtures and finishes to those tile choices when creating concept boards. She created two concepts to help Lauren compare different looks.</p>

3333

3334</div>

3335</div>

3336</div>

3337</div>

3338<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-d-fc-c-c-bacfb">

3340<img class="d-fc-c-c-bacfb-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/ZKqh1R8ZfXYhgQhL4Qu59N6K4Gk5HnC1DecDKW9HY1g/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9mZWF0dXJlZC1kZXNpZ24tcHJvamVjdC1tb2Rlcm4tZmFybWhvdXNlLWJhdGhyb29tLXJlbW9kZWwvY29uY2VwdC1ib2FyZC0xLWZhcm1ob3VzZS1iYXRocm9vbS1yZW1vZGVsLmpwZw" alt="modern farmhouse bathroom remodel concept board 1" title="modern farmhouse bathroom remodel concept board 1"/>

3344<div>

3345<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3346<div>

3347<p>

3348On the first concept board, Martha chose a beautiful black vanity with silver hardware. Though Lauren was open to mixing finishes on the hardware, Martha chose matte black finishes for all the hardware and fixtures in this concept so nothing would compete with the statement silver pulls on the vanity. She wanted Lauren to see how dark elements could pop beautifully against the light walls and tile while still achieving the bright airy feel she wanted.</p>

3349

3353</div>

3356<img class="dacd-cc-ef-ad-db-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/24YEKlOiMIrMAs8bJM0qGbBi-Phv98UEBZmz4UFpDCw/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9mZWF0dXJlZC1kZXNpZ24tcHJvamVjdC1tb2Rlcm4tZmFybWhvdXNlLWJhdGhyb29tLXJlbW9kZWwvY29uY2VwdC1ib2FyZC0yLWZhcm1ob3VzZS1iYXRocm9vbS1yZW1vZGVsLnBuZw" alt="modern farmhouse bathroom remodel concept board 2" title="modern farmhouse bathroom remodel concept board 2"/>

3357</div>

3358</div>

3360<div>

3361<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3362<div>

3363<p>

3364On the second concept board, Martha included a white vanity that looked like other white cabinetry that Lauren has throughout her home. She mixed matte black fixtures with gold hardware to show how the contrast could add unique elements to the bathroom.</p>

3365

3366

3367<p>

3368&ldquo;A lot of people are apprehensive about mixing finishes, but I always recommend it,&rdquo; Martha says. &ldquo;I think it adds a lot more visual interest, and then you&rsquo;re not limited by trying to find every fixture with the exact same finish.&rdquo; Martha chose a freestanding bathtub for both concepts.</p>

3413Before Lauren committed to new products for her new bathroom, Martha helped Lauren better visualize the space by creating a 3D rendering. Though a concept board gives an idea of how the different finishes and fixtures will look together, the 3D rendering allowed Lauren to see exactly how her bathroom would look after remodeling.</p>

3414

3415

3416<p>

3417Additionally, the 3D rendering gave Lauren an idea of how her new fixtures would look in proportion to the rest of the room. One of Lauren&rsquo;s biggest worries was whether the bathtub would fit in the space as planned. The 3D rendering cleared up all her concerns!</p>

3492<h3>

3493Selecting Products</h3>

3494

3495

3496<p>

3497After viewing both the concept board and 3D rendering of the space, Lauren was ready to order products for her modern farmhouse bathroom remodel.</p>

3498

3499

3500<p>

3501Ultimately, Lauren loved the first concept board. &ldquo;I never planned on having any nickel brushes in the bathroom,&rdquo; she says. &ldquo;My go-to hardware combo is black and brass! But when Martha suggested the Wesley vanity, I knew right away it was the right choice. The light fixtures she suggested tied it all together with the rest of the black fixtures. So smart!&rdquo;</p>

4201<h2>

4202DIY Pro-Tip: Work with a Vevano Designer</h2>

4203

4204

4205<p>

4206Vevano designers are a DIYer&rsquo;s best friend! Even with great DIY skills, consulting with an expert can help you have the best outcome possible. Designers like Martha can help you fully visualize your changes before making a full commitment. Their guidance can help you avoid delays in your remodel and making costly mistakes&mdash;meaning you can finish your upgrades on time and under budget.</p>

4207

4208

4209<p>

4210Plus, when you work with a Vevano Home designer, any products you purchase from Vevano Home are deducted from your retainer&mdash;essentially making your design free! Reach out to our designers today for a free consultation on your next home project.</p>
